***selderie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:selderie.html>selderie</a> (67525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">céleri</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">selīnum</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σέλῑνον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sélīnon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>For</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> epenthetic <i><a href = vnd.unilang:d.html>d</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> productive <a href = vnd.unilang:well.html>well</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:into.html>into</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> seventeenth <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kelder.html>kelder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zolder.html>zolder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">daalder</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulder.html>mulder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vilder.html>vilder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">volder</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:senator.html>senator</a> (1675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senātor</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senex</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>old</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:new.html>New</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēpticus</i> + <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:new.html>New</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-emia</i>.

***seraph.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a> (63052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Back-formation <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> singular <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seraphim</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">seraphim</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שרפים</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">serafim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שרף</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">saraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> plural "seraphims" occurs <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:king.html>King</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:james.html>James</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bible.html>Bible</a> (Isaiah <a href = vnd.unilang:chapter.html>chapter</a> 6).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oxford.html>Oxford</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dictionary.html>Dictionary</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> singular "<a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:may.html>may</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:have.html>have</a> originated <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="w:John Milton"><a href = vnd.unilang:john.html>John</a> Milton</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:who.html>who</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:used.html>used</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:book.html>Book</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:i.html>I</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Paradise Lost"><a href = vnd.unilang:paradise.html>Paradise</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a></a> (1667).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:seraph.html>seraph</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphs</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphim</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">seraphims</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biblical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> six-winged <a href = vnd.unilang:angel.html>angel</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> highest choir <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:order.html>order</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:angels.html>angels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:christian.html>Christian</a> angelology, ranked <a href = vnd.unilang:above.html>above</a> cherubim, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:below.html>below</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:they.html>They</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 5th highest <a href = vnd.unilang:order.html>order</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:angels.html>angels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> Jewish angelology. <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:detailed.html>detailed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:description.html>description</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:found.html>found</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beginning.html>beginning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Bible_%28World_English%29/IsaiahChapter_6">Isaiah <a href = vnd.unilang:chapter.html>chapter</a> 6</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:serieus.html>serieus</a> (836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
